<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-care-for-adhd">NURSING CARE FOR ADHD<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-care-for-adhd" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="eating-disorders">EATING DISORDERS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#eating-disorders" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>

379</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="eating-disorders">EATING DISORDERS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#eating-disorders" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>For many, eating symbolizes parental nurturing – the love and care that are the prototype of and a basis for all future intimate relationships</li>
<li>For some, however, eating creates anxiety because of its association with unsatisfactory and unpleasant parent-child interactions.</li>
<li>Clearly, food and eating have greater individual and cultural meaning and importance than merely an activity undertaken to sustain life.</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
380</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="anorexia-nervosa">ANOREXIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#anorexia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
381</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="anorexia-nervosa">ANOREXIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#anorexia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>This is a life-threatening eating disorder characterized by:</li>
<li>the client’s refusal or, inability to maintain a minimally normal body weight</li>
<li>intense fear of gaining weight or becoming fat</li>
<li>significantly disturbed perception of the shape or size of the body</li>
<li>steadfast inability or refusal to acknowledge the seriousness of the problem or even that one exists</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
382</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="anorexia-nervosa">ANOREXIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#anorexia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Clients with anorexia nervosa have:</li>
<li>A body weight that is 85% less than expected for their age and height</li>
<li>Experienced amenorrhea for at least three consecutive cycles</li>
<li>A preoccupation with food and food-related activities</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
383</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="signs-and-symptoms-of-anorexia-nervosa">SIGNS AND SYMPTOMS OF ANOREXIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#signs-and-symptoms-of-anorexia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Fear of gaining weight or becoming fat even when severely underweight (Main Sign)</li>
<li>Body image disturbance</li>
<li>Amenorrhea</li>
<li>Depressive symptoms such as depressed mood, social withdrawal, irritability, and insomnia</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
384</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="signs-and-symptoms-of-anorexia-nervosa">SIGNS AND SYMPTOMS OF ANOREXIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#signs-and-symptoms-of-anorexia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Preoccupation with thoughts of food</li>
<li>Feelings of ineffectiveness</li>
<li>Inflexible thinking</li>
<li>Strong need to control the environment</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
385</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="signs-and-symptoms-of-anorexia-nervosa">SIGNS AND SYMPTOMS OF ANOREXIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#signs-and-symptoms-of-anorexia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Limited spontaneity and overly restrained emotional expression</li>
<li>Complaints of constipation and abdominal pain</li>
<li>Cold intolerance</li>
<li>Lethargy</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
386</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="signs-and-symptoms-of-anorexia-nervosa">SIGNS AND SYMPTOMS OF ANOREXIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#signs-and-symptoms-of-anorexia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Emaciation</li>
<li>Hypotension, hypothermia and bradycardia</li>
<li>Hypertrophy of salivary glands</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
387</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="signs-and-symptoms-of-anorexia-nervosa">SIGNS AND SYMPTOMS OF ANOREXIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#signs-and-symptoms-of-anorexia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Elevated BUN</li>
<li>Electrolyte imbalances</li>
<li>Leukopenia and mild anemia</li>
<li>Elevated liver function studies</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
388</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="bulimia-nervosa">BULIMIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#bulimia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Is an eating disorder characterized by:</li>
<li>Recurrent episodes (at least twice a week for 3 months) of binge eating (consuming a large amount of food, far greater than most people eat at a time, in a discrete period of usually 2 hours or less)</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
389</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="bulimia-nervosa">BULIMIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#bulimia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Is an eating disorder characterized by:</li>
<li>Binge eating followed by inappropriate compensatory behaviors to avoid weight gain such as:</li>
<li>Purging (compensatory behavior designed to eliminate food by means of self-induced vomiting, misuse of laxatives, enemas, and diuretics)</li>
<li>Fasting</li>
<li>Excessively exercising</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
390</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="signs-and-symptoms-of-bulimia-nervosa">SIGNS AND SYMPTOMS OF BULIMIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#signs-and-symptoms-of-bulimia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Recurrent episodes of binge eating</li>
<li>Compensatory behavior such as self-induced vomiting, misuse of laxatives, diuretics, enema or other medications, or excessive exercise</li>
<li>Self-evaluation overly influenced by body shape and weight</li>
<li>Usually within normal weight range, possible underweight or overweight</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
391</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="signs-and-symptoms-of-bulimia-nervosa">SIGNS AND SYMPTOMS OF BULIMIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#signs-and-symptoms-of-bulimia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Restriction of total calorie consumption between binges, selecting low-calorie foods while avoiding foods perceived to be fattening are likely to trigger a binge</li>
<li>Depressive and anxiety symptoms</li>
<li>Possible substance use involving alcohol or stimulants</li>
<li>Loss of dental enamel</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
392</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="signs-and-symptoms-of-bulimia-nervosa">SIGNS AND SYMPTOMS OF BULIMIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#signs-and-symptoms-of-bulimia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Chipped, ragged, or moth eaten appearance of the teeth</li>
<li>Increased dental caries</li>
<li>Menstrual irregularities</li>
<li>Dependence on laxatives</li>
<li>Esophageal tears</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
393</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="signs-and-symptoms-of-bulimia-nervosa">SIGNS AND SYMPTOMS OF BULIMIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#signs-and-symptoms-of-bulimia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Fluid and electrolyte abnormalities</li>
<li>Metabolic alkalosis (from vomiting) or metabolic acidosis (from diarrhea)</li>
<li>Mildly elevated serum amylase levels</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
394</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="risk-factors-for-eating-disorders">RISK FACTORS FOR EATING DISORDERS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#risk-factors-for-eating-disorders" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<table><thead><tr><th>DISORDER</th><th>BIOLOGIC RISK FACTORS</th><th>DEVELOPMENTAL RISK FACTORS</th><th>FAMILY RISK FACTORS</th><th>SOCIO-CULTURAL RISK FACTORS</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Anorexia Nervosa</td><td>Obesity; dieting at an early age</td><td>Issues of developing autonomy and having control over self and environment; developing a unique identity; dissatisfaction with body image</td><td>Family lacks emotional support; parental maltreatment; cannot deal with conflict</td><td>Cultural ideal of being thin; media focus on beauty, thinness, fitness, preoccupation with achieving the ideal body</td></tr><tr><td>Bulimia Nervosa</td><td>Obesity; early dieting; possible serotonin and norepinephrine disturbances; chromosome 1 susceptibility</td><td>Self-perceptions of being overweight, fat, unattractive, and undesirable; dissatisfaction with body image</td><td>Chaotic family with loose boundaries; parental maltreatment including possible physical or sexual abuse</td><td>Same with above, weight-related teasing</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
395</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="common-nursing-diagnoses-related-to-eating-disorders">COMMON NURSING DIAGNOSES RELATED TO EATING DISORDERS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#common-nursing-diagnoses-related-to-eating-disorders" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Body image disturbance</li>
<li>Self-esteem disturbance</li>
<li>Ineffective individual coping</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
396</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions-for-anorexia-nervosa">NURSING INTERVENTIONS FOR ANOREXIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions-for-anorexia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Promote improved nutrition – assume a calm, matter-of-fact attitude and positive expectation of the client, meeting minimal nutritional goals is non-negotiable.</li>
<li>Tube or IV feedings</li>
<li>Weigh daily, record intake and output, observe client during meals and bathroom activities</li>
<li>Avoid discussing food, recipes, restaurants and eating</li>
<li>Provide a pleasant meal time environment and adopt realistic expectations of how much the client will eat</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
397</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions-for-anorexia-nervosa">NURSING INTERVENTIONS FOR ANOREXIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions-for-anorexia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Promote improved nutrition</li>
<li>Frequent, small meals are more acceptable</li>
<li>Set time limit of about one-half hour to forestall mealtime "marathon" (protracted meals during which the client eats little)</li>
<li>Collaborate with a dietitian</li>
<li>Acknowledge and recognize efforts of clients who meet weight gain goals but avoid praise or flattery</li>
<li>Behavior modification therapy can help</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
398</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions-for-anorexia-nervosa">NURSING INTERVENTIONS FOR ANOREXIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions-for-anorexia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Promote effective individual coping</li>
<li>The best way is to involve the clients in their own treatment planning</li>
<li>Give clients the opportunity to practice problem solving. Demonstrate positive belief in client's abilities to regain healthy functioning and a willingness to tolerate "mistakes"</li>
<li>Set firm, clear limits to provide the secure environment needed to learn more effective coping behaviors</li>
<li>Explore client's feelings about their families, their roles in the family and their autonomy within the family system</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
399</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions-for-bulimia-nervosa">NURSING INTERVENTIONS FOR BULIMIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions-for-bulimia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Promoting effective coping with anxiety – help them recognize events that create anxiety and to avoid binging and purging in response to anxiety</li>
<li>Promoting improved fluid volume</li>
<li>Promoting effective individual coping</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
400</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-interventions-for-bulimia-nervosa">NURSING INTERVENTIONS FOR BULIMIA NERVOSA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions-for-bulimia-nervosa" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Promoting effective individual coping</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>It is important for clients to identify situations or patterns of events that precede episodes of binging and purging.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>They need to learn effective ways of expressing feelings and assertive techniques to diminish guilt interactions in the future</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Promoting effective family coping</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
401</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sexual-disorders">SEXUAL DISORDERS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sexual-disorders" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="other-forms-of-paraphilia-partialism">OTHER FORMS OF PARAPHILIA PARTIALISM<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#other-forms-of-paraphilia-partialism" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Inserting the penis into the other parts of the body</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
425</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="type-of-therapy-performed-on-patients-with-paraphilias">TYPE OF THERAPY PERFORMED ON PATIENTS WITH PARAPHILIAS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#type-of-therapy-performed-on-patients-with-paraphilias" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Behavior Modification</li>
<li>A therapeutic intervention involving the application of learning principles in order to change maladaptive behavior</li>
<li>A method of attempting to strengthen a desired behavior or response by reinforcement, either positive or negative</li>
<li>Positive reinforcement is given to the client who exhibits the desired behavior</li>
<li>Negative reinforcement involves removing a stimulus immediately after a (positive) behavior occurs so that the behavior is more likely to occur again</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
426</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="type-of-therapy-performed-on-patients-with-paraphilias">TYPE OF THERAPY PERFORMED ON PATIENTS WITH PARAPHILIAS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#type-of-therapy-performed-on-patients-with-paraphilias" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Aversion Therapy</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>An example of behavior modification in which a painful stimulus is introduced to bring about avoidance of another stimulus with the end view of facilitating behavioral change</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Token Economy</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>An example of behavior modification technique which utilizes the principle of rewarding desired behavior to facilitate change.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
427</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sexual-addiction">SEXUAL ADDICTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sexual-addiction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The frequency of sexual activity can be viewed on a continuum, with most people falling in the middle range</li>
<li>Some have sex frequently in a way that enhances their lives; others have sex infrequently and report contentment and satisfaction</li>
<li>A sexual pattern that falls at either extreme of the continuum, however can signal problems.</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
428</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sexual-addiction">SEXUAL ADDICTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sexual-addiction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Is a disorder in which the central focus of life is sex</li>
<li>People with these addictions spend 50% or more of all waking hours dealing with sex, from fantasy to acting out behavior.</li>
<li>Acting out behavior is often victimless, e.g., overindulging in masturbation, fetishism, pornography use, or commercial telephone sex; or visiting prostitutes</li>
<li>Victimizing behaviors (those with a non-consenting partner) are less frequent and include obscene phone calls, frotturism, voyeurism, exhibitionism, child sexual abuse and rape</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
429</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sexual-addiction">SEXUAL ADDICTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sexual-addiction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Sexual addiction is not simply the frequent enjoyment of sexual behaviors; rather, it is a progressive disease in which sex is used to numb pain.</li>
<li>The pay off is the same as in any other addiction, i.e., an intensely pleasurable, short-lived release from pain, and an escape from the problems of daily life.</li>
<li>The consequences are the same in the addict's life and eventually becomes unmanageable</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
430</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sexual-addiction">SEXUAL ADDICTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sexual-addiction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Many sexual addicts grew up in homes where they were emotionally, physically, or sexually abused</li>
<li>Most of them suffer from low self-esteem and believe themselves unlovable.</li>
<li>They have desperate need for love and they equate sex with proof of love.</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
431</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sexual-addiction">SEXUAL ADDICTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sexual-addiction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The components have the hallmarks of obsessive-compulsive behavior:</li>
<li>Preoccupation</li>
<li>Spends hours thinking or obsessing about sex and is so time consuming that the person cannot fulfill work, school, or family responsibilities</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sexual-addiction">SEXUAL ADDICTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sexual-addiction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The components have the hallmarks of obsessive-compulsive behavior:</li>
<li>Ritualization</li>
<li>The individual engages in specific behaviors done just the “right” way and in the same sequence at the right time. The ritual seems to control anxiety; once addicts begin a ritual, they cannot stop until the cycle is completed</li>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sexual-addiction">SEXUAL ADDICTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sexual-addiction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The components have the hallmarks of obsessive-compulsive behavior:</li>
<li>Compulsivity</li>
<li>The individual cannot control sexual behavior and this behavior becomes the most important aspect of life</li>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sexual-addiction">SEXUAL ADDICTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sexual-addiction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>

Like other addicts, these individuals want to stop their behavior, promise to stop, try to stop and are unable to stop without treatment.</li>

<li>A method of attempting to strengthen a desired behavior or response by reinforcement, either positive or negative</li>
<li>Positive reinforcement is given to the client who exhibits the desired behavior</li>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sexual-dysfunctions">SEXUAL DYSFUNCTIONS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sexual-dysfunctions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>These are <strong>problems or difficulties with sexual expression</strong> classified according to the phase of the sexual response cycle that is affected</li>
<li>This does not include dissatisfaction problems</li>
<li><strong>Contributory factors</strong> actually implicate past and current factors:</li>
<li>Lack of sex education</li>
<li>Internalization of the teaching that sex is dirty or sinful</li>
<li>Parental punishment for normal exploration of one’s genitals</li>
<li>Severe trauma such as rape or child sexual abuse</li>
</ul>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sexual-dysfunctions">SEXUAL DYSFUNCTIONS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sexual-dysfunctions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>

<li>Negative feelings like guilt anxiety, anger which interfere with the ability to experience pleasure and joy</li>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sexual-dysfunction">SEXUAL DYSFUNCTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sexual-dysfunction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="classifications-of-sexual-dysfunction">CLASSIFICATIONS OF SEXUAL DYSFUNCTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#classifications-of-sexual-dysfunction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>

<li>Disorders of Sexual Desire</li>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="disorders-of-sexual-desire">DISORDERS OF SEXUAL DESIRE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#disorders-of-sexual-desire" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Inhibited Sexual Desire</li>
<li>Persistently low interest or a total lack of interest in sexual activity</li>
<li>Sexual Aversion Disorder</li>
<li>Severe distaste for sexual activity or the thought of the sexual activity, which then leads to a phobic avoidance of sex</li>
<li>The most common cause of sexual aversion disorder is childhood sexual abuse or adult rape</li>
<li>Increased Sexual Interest</li>
<li>Symptomatic of the manic phase of a bipolar disorder</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
441</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="arousal-disorders">AROUSAL DISORDERS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#arousal-disorders" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Physiologic responses and subjective sense of excitement experienced during sexual activity</li>
<li>Female Sexual Arousal Disorder</li>
<li>Lack of vaginal lubrication</li>
<li>Male Sexual Arousal Disorder</li>
<li>Occurs when the man has erection problems during 25% or more of sexual interactions; cannot attain a full erection or loses erection prior to orgasm (impotence / erectile inhibition)</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
442</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="orgasm-disorders">ORGASM DISORDERS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#orgasm-disorders" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Inhibited Female Orgasm / Frigid</li>
<li>Woman is totally incapable of responding sexually</li>
<li>Sexual response stops before orgasm occurs</li>
<li>Pre-orgasmic</li>
<li>Women who have never experienced an orgasm</li>
<li>Secondarily Non-Orgasmic</li>
<li>They have had orgasm in the past but are not currently experiencing them</li>
<li>Situationally Non-orgasmic</li>
<li>Have orgasms in some situations but not in others</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
443</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="orgasm-disorders">ORGASM DISORDERS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#orgasm-disorders" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Inhibited Male Orgasm</li>
<li>Male can maintain an erection for long periods (e.g., an hour or more) but has extreme difficulty ejaculating</li>
<li>Could be organic, e.g., spinal cord injuries, multiple sclerosis, due to drugs or may be psychogenic (fear of pregnancy, performance pressure, fear of losing control, anxiety and guilt about engaging in sexual activity)</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
444</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="orgasm-disorders">ORGASM DISORDERS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#orgasm-disorders" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Rapid Ejaculation</li>
<li>One of the most common dysfunction among men</li>
<li>Refers to the absence of voluntary control of ejaculation</li>
<li>Probably due to:</li>
<li>Inability to perceive his arousal level accurately</li>
<li>Lowered sensory threshold due to infrequent sexual activity</li>
<li>Early conditioning as a result of hurried masturbation or hurried sexual intercourse</li>
<li>Extreme anxiety during sexual interaction, resulting in ejaculation triggered by the SNS</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
445</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sexual-pain-disorders">SEXUAL PAIN DISORDERS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sexual-pain-disorders" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Vaginismus</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Involuntary spasms of the outer one third of the vaginal muscles making penetration of the vagina painful and sometimes impossible.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Cause is mainly psychophysiologic: as protection against real or imagined pain; history of sexual trauma; emotional conflict</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
446</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="sexual-pain-disorders">SEXUAL PAIN DISORDERS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#sexual-pain-disorders" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>

<li>Pain during or immediately after intercourse</li>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="problems-with-sexual-satisfaction">PROBLEMS WITH SEXUAL SATISFACTION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#problems-with-sexual-satisfaction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>These are more related to the emotional tone of the relationship than the physiologic response</li>
<li>May be situational, due to lack of extragenital satisfaction, related to the relationship difficulties, due to lack of intimacy</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-care-for-sexual-dysfunctions">NURSING CARE FOR SEXUAL DYSFUNCTIONS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-care-for-sexual-dysfunctions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Reduce anxiety and fear</li>
<li>Accurate identification of feelings is the first step</li>
<li>Help the client identify one anxiety-producing situation within their sexual interactions</li>
<li>The nurse and client may analyze the situation to discover negative anticipatory thoughts that may be the source of the anxiety.</li>
<li>Review how the client has handled anxiety in the past and evaluate the range and effectiveness of this past coping behavior, then explore alternative coping behaviors</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
449</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-care-for-sexual-dysfunctions">NURSING CARE FOR SEXUAL DYSFUNCTIONS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-care-for-sexual-dysfunctions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Decrease spiritual distress</li>
<li>Because the origin of spiritual distress is the lack of intimacy or connection within a sexual relationship, the goal of nursing care is to help clients achieve and maintain a level of intimacy each partner finds comfortable</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
450</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-care-for-sexual-dysfunctions">NURSING CARE FOR SEXUAL DYSFUNCTIONS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-care-for-sexual-dysfunctions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Promote more effective family coping</li>
<li>Apart from setting specific times to share feelings, and belief, some couples need training in more effective communication skills.</li>
<li>Teach couples to avoid the “you” language, which evokes a defensive response and results in arguments, and encourage use of the “I” language, which expresses personal thoughts, feelings and needs.</li>
<li>Example of “You” language</li>
<li>“You only have sex on your mind. You are a pervert”</li>
<li>Example of “I” language</li>
<li>“I am concerned because we seem to have different expectations of how often we would like to make love.”</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
451</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-care-for-sexual-dysfunctions">NURSING CARE FOR SEXUAL DYSFUNCTIONS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-care-for-sexual-dysfunctions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Promote comfort with personal identity</li>
<li>A multidisciplinary approach is most effective in helping transsexuals adjust to their situation</li>
<li>Family and friends need support and counseling to reintegrate this person into their lives as a person of the other sex</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-care-for-sexual-dysfunctions">NURSING CARE FOR SEXUAL DYSFUNCTIONS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-care-for-sexual-dysfunctions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="schizophrenia">SCHIZOPHRENIA.<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#schizophrenia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="schizophrenia">SCHIZOPHRENIA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#schizophrenia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>There is disharmony between the patient's thinking, feeling and acting.</li>
<li>Schizophrenia causes distorted and bizarre thoughts, perceptions, emotions, movements and behavior.</li>
<li>It cannot be defined as a single illness; rather it is thought of as a syndrome or disease process with many different varieties and symptoms</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
461</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="schizophrenia">SCHIZOPHRENIA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#schizophrenia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The main problem in schizophrenia is Altered Thought Process</li>
<li>The most acceptable theory on the cause of schizophrenia is the Biologic Theory which says that schizophrenia is due to</li>
<li>increased dopamine.</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
462</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="characteristics-of-patients-with-schizophrenia">CHARACTERISTICS OF PATIENTS WITH SCHIZOPHRENIA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#characteristics-of-patients-with-schizophrenia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Patients are usually of the asthenic or slender, lightly muscled body type</li>
<li>They tend to be introverted, deficient in their affective response ability, self conscious, retiring, moody and sensitive</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
463</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="characteristics-of-patients-with-schizophrenia">CHARACTERISTICS OF PATIENTS WITH SCHIZOPHRENIA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#characteristics-of-patients-with-schizophrenia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>There is failure in adapting to objective reality.</li>
<li>They usually utilize the mechanism of denial and withdraw from reality.</li>
<li>The patient's abstract ability becomes impaired.</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
464</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="characteristics-of-patients-with-schizophrenia">CHARACTERISTICS OF PATIENTS WITH SCHIZOPHRENIA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#characteristics-of-patients-with-schizophrenia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Patient acts out in ways which would ordinarily be subject to social restraint</li>
<li>Delusions and hallucinations are accessory symptoms.</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
465</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="types-of-schizophrenia">TYPES OF SCHIZOPHRENIA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#types-of-schizophrenia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Paranoid Type</li>
<li>Catatonic Type</li>
<li>Disorganized Type</li>
<li>Undifferentiated Type</li>
<li>Residual Type</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
466</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="schizophrenia-paranoid-type">SCHIZOPHRENIA:-PARANOID TYPE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#schizophrenia-paranoid-type" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Characterized by:</li>
<li>persecutory (feeling victimized or spied on)</li>
<li>Grandiose delusions,</li>
<li>Hallucinations, and occasionally, excessive</li>
<li>Religiosity (delusional religious focus) or</li>
<li>Hostile and aggressive behavior.</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
467</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="schizophrenia-catatonic-type">SCHIZOPHRENIA CATATONIC TYPE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#schizophrenia-catatonic-type" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Characterized by marked psychomotor disturbance, either motionless or excessive motor activity.</li>
<li>Motor immobility may be manifested by catalepsy (waxy flexibility) or stupor</li>
<li>Excessive motor activity is apparently purposeless and is not influenced by external stimuli</li>
<li>Other features include negativism, mutism, peculiarities of voluntary movement, echolalia, and echopraxia</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
468</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="schizophrenia-catatonic-type">SCHIZOPHRENIA CATATONIC TYPE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#schizophrenia-catatonic-type" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>Catatonic Stupor</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Marked decrease in reactivity to the environment and/or reduction in spontaneous movement and activity or mutism</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Catatonic Negativism</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Apparently motive-less resistance to all instruction or attempts to be moved</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Catatonic Rigidity</strong></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Maintenance of a rigid posture against efforts to be moved</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
469</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="schizophrenia-catatonic-type">SCHIZOPHRENIA CATATONIC TYPE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#schizophrenia-catatonic-type" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Catatonic Excitement</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Excited motor activity, apparently purposeless and not influenced by external stimuli</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Catatonic Posturing</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Voluntary assumption of inappropriate posture.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
470</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="schizophrenia-disorganized-type">SCHIZOPHRENIA DISORGANIZED TYPE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#schizophrenia-disorganized-type" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Incoherence, marked loosening of associations, or grossly disorganized behavior</li>
<li>Flat or grossly inappropriate affect</li>
<li>Does not meet the criteria for the catatonic type</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
471</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="schizophrenia-undifferentiated-type">SCHIZOPHRENIA UNDIFFERENTIATED TYPE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#schizophrenia-undifferentiated-type" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Characterized by mixed schizophrenic symptoms (of other types) along with disturbances of thought, affect and behavior</li>
<li>Prominent delusions, hallucinations, incoherence or grossly disorganized behavior</li>
<li>Patients whose manifestations cannot be fitted into one or the other types</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
472</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="schizophrenia-residual-type">SCHIZOPHRENIA RESIDUAL TYPE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#schizophrenia-residual-type" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Absence of prominent delusions, hallucinations, incoherence or grossly disorganized behavior</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
473</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="schizophrenia-residual-type">SCHIZOPHRENIA RESIDUAL TYPE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#schizophrenia-residual-type" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Continuing evidence of the disturbance, as indicated by 2 or more of these residual symptoms:</li>
<li>Marked social isolation or withdrawal</li>
<li>Marked impairment in role functioning as wage-earner, student or homemaker</li>
<li>Marked peculiar behaviors</li>
<li>Marked impairment in personal hygiene and grooming</li>
<li>Odd beliefs or magical thinking, influencing behavior and inconsistent with cultural norms.</li>
<li>Marked lack of initiative, interest</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
474</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="criteria-for-prognosis-of-schizophrenia">CRITERIA FOR PROGNOSIS OF SCHIZOPHRENIA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#criteria-for-prognosis-of-schizophrenia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Favorable Prognosis</li>
<li>Good socialization</li>
<li>Late / acute onset</li>
<li>Adequate support system</li>
<li>Family history of mood disorder</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
476</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="criteria-for-prognosis-of-schizophrenia">CRITERIA FOR PROGNOSIS OF SCHIZOPHRENIA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#criteria-for-prognosis-of-schizophrenia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Unfavorable Prognosis</li>
<li>Poor / no socialization</li>
<li>Early and insidious onset</li>
<li>Few / no support system</li>
<li>History of chronicity / many relapses</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
477</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="fundamental-signs-and-symptoms-of-schizophrenia-as-identified-by-bleuler">FUNDAMENTAL SIGNS AND SYMPTOMS OF SCHIZOPHRENIA AS IDENTIFIED BY BLEULER<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#fundamental-signs-and-symptoms-of-schizophrenia-as-identified-by-bleuler" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Associative Looseness</li>
<li>Autism</li>
<li>Apathy</li>
<li>Ambivalence</li>
</ul>
<p>4 A’s</p>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
478</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="symptoms-of-schizophrenia">SYMPTOMS OF SCHIZOPHRENIA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#symptoms-of-schizophrenia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>The symptoms of schizophrenia are divided into two major categories:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Positive or hard symptoms / signs, which include delusions, hallucinations, and grossly disorganized thinking, speech and behavior</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Negative or soft symptoms / signs such as blunting, avolition, and social withdrawal or discomfort</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
479</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="negative-or-soft-symptoms-of-schizophrenia">NEGATIVE OR SOFT SYMPTOMS OF SCHIZOPHRENIA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#negative-or-soft-symptoms-of-schizophrenia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Alogia</li>
<li>Catatonia</li>
<li>Anhedonia</li>
<li>Flat Affect</li>
<li>Apathy</li>
<li>Lack of Volition</li>
<li>Blunted Affect</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
480</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="general-signs-and-symptoms-of-schizophrenia">GENERAL SIGNS AND SYMPTOMS OF SCHIZOPHRENIA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#general-signs-and-symptoms-of-schizophrenia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ol>
<li>Perceptual changes</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>May occur in all the senses or not.</li>
</ul>
<p>1a) Illusions</p>
<ul>
<li>Client's misperceives or exaggerates stimuli in the external environment</li>
</ul>
<p>1b) Hallucinations (hallmark of schizophrenia)</p>
<ul>
<li>May be visual, olfactory, gustatory, tactile, or auditory</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
481</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="delusions">DELUSIONS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#delusions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Disturbances in the content rather than the form of thought</li>
<li>Fixed false beliefs about one's environment or event occurring in it</li>
<li>Types of delusions</li>
<li>Persecutory or Paranoid Delusions</li>
<li>Grandiose Delusions</li>
<li>Religious Delusions</li>
<li>Somatic Delusions</li>
<li>Referential Delusions or Ideas of Reference</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
482</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="general-signs-and-symptoms-of-schizophrenia">GENERAL SIGNS AND SYMPTOMS OF SCHIZOPHRENIA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#general-signs-and-symptoms-of-schizophrenia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ol start="2">
<li>Disturbances in thought</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>The thinking is unclear</li>
<li>Thoughts are disconnected or disjointed</li>
<li>Examples:
2a) Clang Associations
2b) Delusions</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
483</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="general-signs-and-symptoms-of-schizophrenia">GENERAL SIGNS AND SYMPTOMS OF SCHIZOPHRENIA<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#general-signs-and-symptoms-of-schizophrenia" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ol start="3">
<li>Changes in communication</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>Clients have difficulty responding appropriately to events and people they encounter because of their distorted perceptions.</li>
<li>Examples:
3a) Thought Disorganization
3b) Thought Blocking
3c) Tangential Communication
3d) Circumstantial Communication
3e) Alogia</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
484</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="thought-disorganization">THOUGHT DISORGANIZATION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#thought-disorganization" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Responses are inappropriate to the situation</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
485</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="thought-blocking">THOUGHT BLOCKING<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#thought-blocking" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Clients may suddenly stop talking in the middle of a sentence and remain silent for several seconds to one minute</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
486</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="tangential-thinking">TANGENTIAL THINKING<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#tangential-thinking" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Veering into unrelated topics and never answering the original question</li>
</ul>
<p>Mr. Vincent Ejakait
487</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="circumstantial-communication">CIRCUMSTANTIAL COMMUNICATION<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#circumstantial-communication" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
